Dirty lashes = unhealthy lashes 😷🤢
_
Piger... Det er også vigtigt at pleje sine vipper. Ukorrekt pleje vil forårsage mere hår tab, usunde og kortere vipper.
_
Da eyelash extensions bliver pålagt ens egne naturvipper, er det en god ting at vaske vipperne - specielt hvis man går med makeup til dagligt, eller har tendens til meget søvn omkring øjnene.
_
Vipperne bliver nemlig påvirket af snavs og de får ikke den rette mulighed for, at vokse sig lange og naturlige som de plejer og det vil derfor være en forudsætning for eyelash extensions.
_
I kan købe pleje produkter, gennem mig til en billigere pris. Der findes også andre alternativer. Spørg endelig hvis I skulle blive i tvivl 🤗❤️

What is it Antipasto? 💭🤔 .
.
🔹🔸 (plural antipasti) is the traditional first course of a formal Italian meal. .
.
🔸🔹Typical ingredients of a traditional antipasto include cured meats, olives, peperoncini, mushrooms, anchovies, artichoke hearts, various cheeses (such as provolone or mozzarella), pickled meats, and vegetables in oil or vinegar. .
.
🔹🔸 Whats not to like? 🇮🇹😋

Are you ready for the new week? We sure are! 🛍️ Come and say hi! 👋

🤩Perhaps due to its unique sweetness, the most famous and appreciated, even abroad, is cipolla di Tropea – onion from Tropea.😋🇮🇹 .
.
🔹WHY SO GOOD? 
Grown by hand on the clay cliffs that descend from Mount Poro towards the sea between Cape Vaticano, Zambrone, Tropea and Briatico, in the provinces of Cosenza and Vibo Valentia, the Tropea onion was brought to Calabria by the Greeks, who had discovered it thanks to the Assyrians and Babylonians. However, it was the Arabs who perfected its cultivation in Tropea, where they settled for some time, and contributed to its spreading through the region.
.
. 🔹THE TASTE 
The shape of its bulbs, of a deep purple color, vary from round to oval to elongated. The onion’s extraordinary sweetness, its delicate scent, its lightness and enjoyable taste, which derive from the morphological peculiarities of the soil and microclimate where it is grown, make it a much sought after ingredient by gourmets and chefs.
.
. 🔹HEALTH BENEFITS
As if its wonderful taste wasn’t enough, the Tropea onion has proven health benefits, known since ancient times. Pliny the Elder, in his “Naturalis Historia”, lists 30 ailments that can be treated with the onion, and medical science has confirmed its healing powers. Recent studies have shown that the Tropea onion, because of its high quality, seem to provide better therapeutic functions than other varieties, especially diuretic, hypoglycemic, and anticancer functions. In addition, it has antiseptic properties, it can alleviate both cold and flu symptoms, it strengthens the cells and tone the arteries, it lowers blood pressure, and it is also used in dermatology. .
. 🔹HOW TO USE
In addition to be eaten raw in salads, the Tropea onion can be prepared in several different ways: baked, boiled, as a filling for frittata (omelette). In Tropea, it is also used to produce a delicious onion marmalade, to be consumed on crostini, as an appetizer and as an accompaniment to roasts. Another delicacy made in Tropea is a marmalade of onion and roasted peppers, a perfect accompaniment for roasts. 😃🇮🇹😋 Stay tuned for the next post, more about all our products and where they are coming from.

💭 Gold from Calabria? 💭 🔸Olive oil: (called: Gold of calabria)

Did you know that almost a quarter of Italy’s olive oil is produced in Calabria? Because Calabria is a well-known for producer. Very often the Calabrian oil is used as a base and mixed with other regions’ oil, then labeled as a product of that region! 🔸In the Calabrian territory, there are three Olive Oils in Denomination of Protected Origin.
Lametia DPO is distinguished by its delicate and fruity taste of medium intensity, low acidity and richness in terms of polyphenols and vitamin E. When tasted, it is wide and balanced, with harmonious notes of unripe tomato and fresh herbs. The spicy and bitter tastes are balanced. It has a variable color from green to straw yellow.
Lametia PDO Extra Virgin Olive Oil is mainly produced in the territories of the province of Catanzaro.
Stay tuned with the next post 🇮🇹😋🤙

Have you ever been in Calabria? 🔹Historical Sites 🔹
Explore Calabria's history with a visit to one of the local UNESCO-designated World Heritage Sites. The Cattolica Monastery in Stilo dates from around the 10th century and is a testament to Stilo's past links to Greece and the Ottoman Empire in the eastern Mediterranean. The tiny red-brick church is built into the mountainside, following a Greek cross layout, and bears many similarities to structures found in Armenia and parts of Greece. Other Byzantine-era religious sites survive in Calabria at Santa Maria del Pathirion in Rossano and San Giovanni Teresti in Bivongi. 🔹Beaches🔹
Most Calabrian visitors head for the coast to enjoy the region's hot summer weather. Regional capital Reggio di Calabria basks in an average of 88 degrees F in August, its hottest, and also busiest, month. The pretty coastal town of Tropea makes a good base for sunseekers with its extensive sandy beaches and views out over the Tyrrhenian Sea as far as Mount Stromboli on a clear day. Nearby, the Capo Vaticano beaches of Grotticelle and Tonicello are large enough to find your own space even during the peak season. 🔹Outdoors Activities🔹
Tourists focus mainly on Calabria's coastline so much of its interior remains relatively undeveloped; agriculture provides the primary source of income in the region. Visit a working farm like Le Pisarre near Cosenza to see fields of citrus and olive trees, and to buy organic fruit, vegetables and honey. To further explore Calabria's landscape, visit the Parco Nazionale Della Sila (parcosila.it/web/en), which takes in areas of Mediterranean scrub land along with pine and beech forests. Hike to the park in spring to see beautiful wildflowers in full bloom, including violi, narcissi and hyacinth alongside edible plants like thyme, oregano and mint. Stay tuned for the next post 🇮🇹😋😍

Have you ever been in Calabria? 🔹The tip of the Italian "boot" is a Region of Southern Italy; it borders to the north with Basilicata and to the south-west the sea separates it from Sicily. 🔹Calabria has a great caratteristic,  the diversity of landscapes and the proximity of the mountains to the sea:  there is always a place from which you can go from the mountain to the sea, reached in a short time. In an hour you can go from 300 to 1000 meters above sea level and from one coast to the other. This, among others, is a spectacular reason of the holiday in this wonderful land, able to satisfy different tastes and needs with a dynamic tourist offer and at the same time a massive relax. 🔹The weather is superb. The Ionian coast is drier and arid than the tirreno which presents a more mild climate. Temperatures generally along the coasts never fall below 10 degrees and never rise above 40 ° C, with peaks of 42-44 ° C in the summer months. Along the Apennines and inland, from Pollino, Sila to Aspromonte, the climate is mountainous Apennines with cold and snowy winters, summer is warm and there is no shortage of thunderstorms.
The main cities are Reggio Calabria, Catanzaro, Lamezia Terme, Cosenza and Crotone.

💭What do you know about APERITIVO?💭 It has been said that the aperitivo concept started in Torino in 1786 by the creator of the vermouth liquor, Antonio Benedetto Carpano
The classic Italian aperitivo drinks differ by region but usually include a mix with Aperol or Campari liquors. They may taste a bit bitter at the first sip, but once you’ve tried them on a couple different occasions, the taste is quite nice
🔸How is serve?
Some bars and restaurants keep it good and simple with a drink, olives and nuts. Others go all out with their food spread, offering different types of fresh pasta, Italian cheeses, grilled or sautéed vegetables, and sandwiches.
The idea is to not make the aperitivo your dinner, but to simply have some finger food with a drink while socializing and stimulating your appetite for dinner.
🔸Cost:
Depending on where you go, the price of an aperitivo usually varies between 5 euros to 15 euros, and includes one drink and an unlimited food buffet. 🔸Time:
The hours for a dinner aperitivo are usually between 6:30-8:30pm. 
Definetly worth to try 😋🇮🇹

Thank you to everyone who came to see Sleeping Beauty! The supportive and engaged audience members, our dedicated and hard-working crew and our talented and enthusiastic cast made for an incredible show that is hard to say goodbye to. 👸💤👋 If you’re feeling the post-show blues too, not to worry! We have new, exciting events and performances coming soon. First up, we have the next Open Stage on 16 February followed by a play reading on 19 February. Next we will be holding auditions for Cabaret on 3-4 March. And don’t forget, our next main stage show, Pride & Prejudice, takes the stage 18-28 April (and tickets are already available)! We can’t wait to see you at one of our events soon. 🎭🎉✨ Photos by Hubert Baumeister

#EshaKhamo - Om keratin treatment 
Keratin behandling er permanent udglatning  og som er verdens første uden formaldehyd, allergener og andre skadelige aldehyder. Ved at produktet ikke indeholder de førnævnte farlige kemiske ingredineser gør, at vores Keratin behandlinger ikke bryder svovlbroerne, men tvæt imod er med til at genopbygge hårestrået og keratinfibrene.
•
•

Keratin behandling er til de, som har problemer med krøllet, kruset, bølget og tykt hår, og som ønsker glat, blankt hår, der føles let. •
•

www.EshaKhamo.dk / 3312 2400 •
•

SPICE SPECIALIST 📃
•
These small black seeds are a common ingredient in the Middle East and India. Nigella seeds are aromatic, slightly bitter and peppery and can be fried before the use to enhance the flavour. They are sometimes used in garam masalas or milder dishes such as kormas.
•
In the Middle East and India, nigella seeds are often added to bread dough before baking.
•

At the doctor’s office today. 
In our grey and cold winter days without sunshine or snow a little extra candles and left over Christmas lighting makes everything better. 
In Copenhagen City many of the medical clinics are quite small and situated in old buildings just as the private apartments. I loved this place because it was quiet and didn’t feel like a medical clinic at all.
The view through this window was to the private backyard - these backyards are often hidden treasures in the city.

Brunch at @madogkaffe is always a good idea, specially when you share it with other foodies that you meet through this amazing community called @instagram 💙
.
Leah @questionably_adulting, her friend and myself shared 3 magnificent brunch plates at one of Copenhagen’s faves.
You have quite a selection of options to choose from. 3 for 89DKK, 5 for 129DKK and 7 for 154DKK
.
Take for example what you see on the photo: fried eggs, organic bread with butter, avocado with toasted almonds, blueberry yoghurt topped off with granola, homemade chicken nugget with sweet n’ sour sauce, Danish cheese with marmalade, salmon, pastries and a long list of mouth-watering etceteras 😋🥐🍳☕️🧀🥖🥗
.
Be prepared to wait in line and to be stared at when taking lots of photos though 🙋🏽‍♂️😌📸
.
Tak for mad my friends, it’s always a pleasure to eat your food ❤️
.

"You must be the laughing Lama" our wonderful guide told me as we walked down the mountain of Tiger's Nest in Bhutan 🇧🇹 back in June 2016.
"Yes, Kristine the Lama comes in many different characters", he continued as I tried to laugh his words of me. 🙏

This laugh is real, I know. Yet despite its sincere and a peace breaker it does affect some people in a less peaceful way. I keep reminding myself that I am me, my laughter is often loud and if it's an issue worth moaning about from other people its none of my business. ☯ +🕉️ =♥ #grounded

A postal card from yesterday’s photo walk in Copenhagen ❤️🇩🇰
I started my day at @madogkaffe having brunch with a couple of fellow foodies that I met through Instagram (how cool is that 😌). A thousand photos later I proceeded to one of my favorite solo hang-out spots and coffee bars @prologcoffeebar.
Right after I found myself at the terrace of Hotel Danmark sipping on a dark cold beer and contemplating the city from above completely alone with the sun warming up my face and nostalgic thoughts.
Of course I got hungry at some point so I walked around the inner city trying to figure out where to munch down my savage appetite.
I stopped at this plaza to shot the people passing by and the pretty colorful buildings.
I ended at @muslingbistro enjoying some nice seafood and local beers, sitting by the window and watching life pass by, wondering when will the day come that I don’t have to leave...
Anyway, dreams and goals -specially when they seem so far away- are what keep me so alive.
I will see you soon Copenhagen. Happy 2018 everybody 🙋🏽‍♂️😌

I denne weekend vil du kunne finde alle @sabinasofia_guldsmed smukke smykker i vores lokaler 💍

Her er lidt om @sabinasofia_guldsmed : "Når jeg sidder bag min guldsmedsbænk, kender duften af brændt støbesand, hører slagene fra hammeren,og ser slagloddet flyde. der finder jeg min inspiration. 
Med stor passion for mit håndværk vil jeg lave smykker som minder os om de øjeblikke vi vil mindes foraltid. 
Jeg vil forevige det øjeblikke han går ned på knæ og hun siger ja, forevige den dag et nyt familiemedlem velkomnes varmt ind i familien. Forevige de øjeblikke vi aldrig vil glemme.
Denne udstilling handler om glæde"

Du vil finde et bredt udvalg af deres nuværende kollektion, og der vil desuden være kollektionsprøver og rester til ekstra gode priser. Det er alletiders chance for at få købt nogle unikke julegaver der både gavner og glæder.

Du vil desuden også kunne høre mere om hvordan @carebyme arbejder i Nepal og Bolivia, og der vil selvfølgeligt også være lidt godt til ganen som kan nydes i vores særligt indrettet julelounge!

ALT dette sker: d. 11., 12. & 13. december kl. 12-19

Skynd dig ned i vores lokaler og find den perfekte julegave eller adventsgave!

I dag er det nemlig sidste gang du opleve @afempire007 i vores lokaler.

De har håndplukket de lækreste accessories, journals, kalendere, vintage kjoler, og tasker, samt smukke kuffert mærker og passport omslag i læder.

De bringer de fineste produkter fra @eccololtd til Danmark for første gang. The World Traveler collection, indeholder smukke kuffert mærker og passport omslag, der gør rejser lidt sjovere. 
Deres notesbøger opfordre til at skrive mere i hånden, være i nuet og blive inspireret til at nedfælde ord og tanker.

Deres filosofi er at shoppe få lækre ting, genbruge og turde flashe det hele. * MOBILEPAY & KONTANT * 📒 #popupshop

This has to be the coolest dorm to live at in Copenhagen for a student! Love these old buildings and all the weird rituals the students practice here. 
And look at that view! #Rundetårn, the round tower at the #Trinitatiskirke build back in the Renaissance. 
Fun fact: the rebus is a mixture of latin and hebrew, and scholars are still today debating what it really means.

Its not only interesting at the sunny side in Nyhavn, take the Courtyard here e.g with not only a first Backyard, but also a second as it where many places in Copenhagen earlier. This way more people could be housed. Back then I imagine rats and dirt was to be found here, but now a days its all been restored and looks amazing in here.
So if you are ever in Nyhavn, you should go see for yourself.

Fra fredag d. 1 december og indtil søndag d. 3 december kan du igen opleve @thomineandartfellow's fantastiske værker i vores lokaler

Udstillingen består både af nyere værker samt Limited edition kunst print i forskellige størrelser, som der vil være mulighed for at købe.

Dørene åbner fredag d. 1 December fra kl 17.00 - 20.00, hvor de første 25 gæster traditionen tro får et gratis Limited edition print i str. A4.

SPICE SPECIALIST 📃
•
The most popular cardamom is green capsules with brown seeds. White cardamom comes from the same plant, but the pods have been bleached for aesthetic reasons. Black cardamom is related to green cardamom, but has very different taste and smoked scent.

Meet Andreas. He is the Store Manager of @cyklistbutikken1905 which is operated by the Danish Cyclists' Federation. I would very much have liked to see how the surroundings looked like back in King Christian IV 'th days. Back then, in the Renaissance, this was his "cottage" and the quite large Kitchengarden which where placed in the park supplied vegetables for the Royal Court. 
If you haven't seen the Castle from inside, you should. Theres so many beautiful items and several fun gadgets. I guess the King was a bit weird.

Lunchin’ a la Italiana in Copenhagen is what I wanna do everyday, all day 😍🇩🇰🇮🇹
.
What a pleasant surprise was to spontaneously visit Spaghetteria La Perla, the first actual Spaghetteria in town.
This time I tried the lunch menu, in which most of their dishes -including pastas and pizzas- are incredibly priced at 79 DKK.
We tried pesto and chicken pasta and a creamy bacon, pea and tomato pasta.
Both substantial, delicious and perfectly cooked 👏🏽
Throw in a couple of Aperol spritzes and life doesn’t get much better than that.
Bon appetit a tutti ❤️🇮🇹!
.

Fra på fredag og indtil søndag kan du opleve @brixsidsel og @hellekjaerulf, billedkunstnere fra henholdsvis Silkeborg og Aarhus.

Sidsel Brix maler akryl på lærred i form af kontraster i streg og flade bygget op i mange tynde varierede skarpe og slørede lag. Dels nonfigurative kompositioner omhandlende ro kontra spænding - med fokus på lys, form og dybe. Dels abstrakte udsigter over temaer som urbane landskaber, industrielle havne og sølandskaber.

Helle Kjærulf maler også akryl på lærred. Abstrakt eller non-figurativt. Det ubevidste og intuitive dominerer i lag på lag i en harmonisk komposition ofte med stor transparens. Naturens foranderlighed afspejler sig i hendes billeder, nogle gange som mentale landskaber, mindscapes.

Vi glæder os til at se dig 🎨

This is the oldest Fountain in Copenhagen, dated back to 1608. Today its standing at a new stocket, but the inside is the original. 💭Funfact: every year at the Queens birthday, golden Apples are jumping up and down in the beam of water.

✨ Dagens kandidat til #KV17: Allan Mylius Thomsen, opstillet i #IndreBy ✨ "Kampen må stadig stå for, at byens borgere får den service som en hovedstad anstændigvis må tilbyde. De ældste kvarterer skal, under hensyntagen til vareleverancer til de mange små næringsdrivende, lukkes for daglig privatkørsel. Yderkvartererne skal indrettes med fokus på de dem der bor der. Vi skal bekæmpe, at kapitalinteresser kan omdanne særlige områder til velhaverkvarterer. Derfor skal vi arbejde for, at der stadig bygges socialt- og almennyttigt boligbyggeri, så priserne ikke presses op på den tilbageværende boligmasse."

Compared with sunshine and blue sky, rain and wind are more representative of Copenhagen. The beauty of the city, however, will not fade away because of the rain. Instead, windy and rainy days bring Copenhagen with freshness. The wisdom of having multi-colored architecture vitalizes the city by looking more like a wet painting rather than a lively scene. 📍Copenhagen , Denmark

A bit of some of the many amazing details on the old library building of Copenhagen University in Inner Copenhagen. This is the main entrance of the building that was build between 1857 and 1861. It's a real gem for brick lovers and supposed to be equally beautiful on the inside. I've never seen it but the peaks I get through the windows tells me it's true. #indreby #delditkbh #mursten #mageløstmurværk #københavnsuniversitet #ku #fiolstræde #fiolstræde1 #universitetsbiblioteket #bricks #ihavethisthingwithbricks

Day 41 / 100 happy days:
Et billede af Torvehallerne her til aften. Det ligger lige ved siden af min arbejdsplads, så jeg går forbi her hver morgen og hver aften. Jeg elsker den stemning, der er i og omkring Torvehallerne - alle fristelserne - de mange anderledes og spændende madvarer, man kan købe derinde - folk, der hygger sig. Alt i alt kan man vist roligt sige, at Torvehallerne blev en meget større succes end først ventet.
Torvehallerne skal have et like fra mig. 👍

#cleansing the #palate #artfreeweek #scenes from #copenhagen #grey #autumn #sky #hotel #church #religion #sktpedersstræde #vorfruekirke set fra/seen from #jarmersplads #københavn #indreby #cross #rentaroom in #gods #house

Once again an example of how you can pass by the same place a hundred times and not see what's right in front of you until one day you all of the sudden realize the beauty of something. In this case the former bank near Nørreport station, on the corner of Købmagergade and Nørre Voldgade. "Den Danske Landmandsbank" means "The Danish Farmer Bank". It was established in 1871 and was quickly grew to be the biggest bank in the North. Today the bank is called Danish Bank and is still the biggest in the country. But the building now houses outlet sales. #nørreport #nørreportstation #dendanskelandmandsbank #danskebank #landmandsbanken #nørrevoldgade #købmagergade #indreby #delditkbh #kigopkbh #mursten #ihavethisthingwithbricks

Ugens mest populære butik til leje 😎
Sandwich/juicebar i pisserenden til leje beliggende 
Larsbjørnsstræde 6, 1454 København K
Butikken er beliggende i et af indre bys mest attraktive og cool områder, kaldet "Pisserenden". Et område der næsten hele døgnet summer af god stemning og kreativitet. Områdets mange populære restauranter, butikker og beværtninger sørger for en altid god strøm at kunder. Butikken er beliggende i den helt gode ende af Larsbjørnsstræde, lige ved hjørnet af Vestergade og meget tæt på Strøget. SPICE SPECIALIST 📃

Rosemary is related to lavender, and its long, tough leaves give a dominant flavour, that can easily overpower a dish. It makes a useful addition to strong meat and game dishes, and a little rosemary can infuse stews and marinades with a powerful aroma.

Copenhagen is world's ninth most expensive city. 🇩🇰 #copenhagen #københavn #facts #fakta #dyr #by #at #leve #i #menvihardetgodt #centrum #udsigt #sommer #indreby

Nørre Voldgade 9, 2. tv., 1358 København K
Kontant: 9.995.000
Kvadratmeter: 184
Værelser: 4

Luksuslejlighed med masser af detaljer

Liebhaveri i topklasse. Fra den åbne entré med biopejs, føres man direkte videre ind i det dejlige køkken-alrum og et helt unikt lysindfald og udsigt. Gulvene er nogle af Københavns længste med længde på 14 meter. Kombineret med en bredde på 45 cm, er gulvene nogle af Københavns flotteste. De er naturligvis fra Dinesen. Det lækre køkken fra Boffi byder på Italienske køkkendrømme midt i København med masser af skabs- og opbevaringsplads samt moderne faciliteter. Alrummet lokker desuden med en TV/sofa-afdeling samt en hyggelig spiseplads hvor biopejsen er gennemgående ud til entréen. Køkken alrummet er på over 80m2 og er lyst og venligt med en fantastisk atmosfære. Udgang til oprindelig balkon hvor udsigten kan nydes over byens puls. Stort lækkert masterbedroom beliggende ned af Vendersgade med indbygget skabsvæg. Endvidere direkte adgang til masterbedrommets egne private badeværelse i Italiensk stil. De flotteste sten på gulv, en lækker marmor bordplade og designer toilet og vask udgør dette badeværelset der er taget ud af et boligmagasin. 2 dejlige værelser med plads til både børn og voksne mod gården. Denne afdeling rummer lejlighedens 2. badeværelse med vaskesøjle, toilet og separat brus. Dette er en skøn storbylejlighed, som især appellerer til yngre par, der ønsker at have det hele ved hånden. Her mærker man storbyens puls, samtidig med, at man har mulighed for at trække sig tilbage. En unik bolig med mange muligheder. #skbolig #TilByen #city #kbhK #indreby #balkon #Boffikøkken #Dinesengulve #hjertetafKøbenhavn #Nørreport #Ørstedsparken #IsraelsPlads #Torvehallerne #Liebhaveri #luksuslejlighed #siesbyekapsch #KØBNU

Klerkegade 2D, 2. th., 1308 København K
Kontant: 8.750.000
Kvadratmeter: 154
Værelser: 4

Citylejlighed i historisk ejendom med altan og elevator i Salomons Palæ. Uden bopælspligt!
Her er virkelig tale om Liebhaveri. Ejendommen er nok en af de smukkeste i City. Boligen er super skarp, og med de rene linjer i denne bolig, kan du ikke ønske mere.

Lejlighedens opgang er via den majestætiske indgang med de smukke søjler. Boligen ligger på anden sal og har med sin indskudte etage, et helt specielt og originalt look. Boligen har et imponerende lyst og meget højloftet opholdsrum med flot integreret JKE køkken. Fra køkken/alrummet er der via en stor entré, trappe op til en charmerende indskudt etage, der er med til at give lejligheden sit helt eget udtryk. Superflot badeværelse med vaskesøjle. Soveværelset i denne bolig er ekstra stort og har direkte adgang til en stor flot altan. Lejligheden er velegnet til enten et par eller en familie med et barn. #skbolig #liebhaveri #salomonspalæ #undenbopælspligt #TilByen #Klerkegade #indreby #city #kbhK #siesbyekapsch #KØBNU

Say hello to our new product 👋
•
SUMAC PEPPER
•
As clean and simple as possible, citrusy and fresh blend
of three ingredients- sumac, black pepper and salt.
•
Since we got many questions about lemon pepper but didn't want to make it the conventional way (with E330, potatoe starch and other unnecessary ingredients) we created something that lives up to ASA standards.
•
Come and try it in Torvehallerne 📌

Brunch at @theunionkitchen had been on my list for such a long time...
Expectations were high, definitely. Based on the looks one might think that it was darn delicious. Yeah, you are right. They did not disappoint!
A menu that goes beyond your typical brunch options but that actually feels like breakfast and lunch items combined and intertwined. Pizza with kale, tomatoes and a fried egg; pulled pork with a poached egg, avocado and tortilla chips; steak and eggs, eggs benedictine, a few salads (that can be adapted to the vegan foodie as well) and I'm sure you get my drift.
You don't? Well, then go and see for yourself😏
A classic selection of cold and warm drinks and a tempting cocktail list round up a menu that is da bomb⭐️!
Why do you think I come back to Copenhagen so often? Well, food is a big big reason😍
P.s. special thanks to @sabrinapatricia for posing and bearing with my maniac need of getting THE best shot. We actually met through Instagram and talked about many things and we both see social media as a platform to connect and inspire💚
Cheers to life, good food, friends and Copenhagen. Ya'll have a grrrreat Wednesday!

Galionsvej 48, 1437 København K
Kontant: 16.995.000
Kvm: 324
Værelser: 6
Townhouse på Holmen med aftensol og smuk udsigt indover byen
Siden 1995, hvor flåden flyttede væk fra Holmen, har området gennemgået en stor forvandling. Magasinerne er i dag indrettet til boliger, hvorfra de nye beboere kan nyde den storslåede udsigt over havnen og dens kanaler, samt det nye operahus.

Wishing to be in Copenhagen right right now eating that delicious food and enjoying life to the fullest.
Not that the Stockholm's food scene isn't great but Copenhagen is definitely another level.
@fars.dreng delivers one of the best brunch experiences in town, with a menu that constitutes only of people-pleaser dishes, fantastic, delicious and so so pretty.
My crew that day consisted of serious foodies and Instagrammers as well, and we were literally the loudest, funniest and coolest table in da house, modesty aside🙈⭐️.
When in Copenhagen make sure to visit this place. And if you haven't been yet to Cph, then may this be one of the reasons for your first visit.
Brunch is served amigos, enjoy and eat as much as you can😍

Coloring my world.

Kronprinsessegade 14B, st., 1306 København K

Kontant: 10.900.000 
248 kvm. 
5 værelser, 2 badeværelser og gårdhave

Liebhaverlejlighed i 2 plan på i alt 248 kvm. BBR i international klasse på byens bedste adresse og med brugsret til egen gårdterrasse

Yderst attraktivt kvarter - omendt det mest eksklusive område i København, lige overfor byens oase, Kongens Have. Kvarteret byder på hyggelige caféer og små spændende specialforretninger. Der er kun få minutters gang til både Strøget og Kongens Nytorv. Efter branden i 1795 anlagdes Kronprinsessegade efter ønske fra kronprinsen, den senere kong Frederik VI (1768-1839)  #skbolig #byensbedsteadresse #liebhaverlejlighed #indreby #kbhK #KongensNytorv #Strøget #Kronprinsessegade #oase #gårdterrasse #KongensHave #siesbyekapsch #KØBNU

Simeons Kirke på Nørrebro, Søndag d. 10. September kl. 16! Hepp! Vi ses!

Selv på en regnfuld dag som i dag tager den smukke museumhave Grønnegården sig flot ud. Haven er gemt lidt væk i indre by, men jeg har arbejdet lige ved siden af og har gjort flittig brug af den (der er fri adgang). I haven finder du denne bænk. Fra bænken har du udsigt til havens smukke lindetræer og hvad haven ellers kan byde på af installationskunst eller møbler, som denne orange sag. Det er her, jeg slår mig ned, når jeg skal dykke ned i en bog. Og det var lige præcis, hvad jeg gjorde her til formiddag. Under en paraply, vel at mærke ☔️ Selvom jeg er ret så glad for byens pulserende kvarterer, så er det rart at kunne koble af i rolige omgivelser - og det kan man blandt andet gøre på en af byens museer eller haver. Ha' en dejlig lørdag 🙋🏻 /Medine @medineduvarci

#lifeindenmark #wonderfulcopenhagen #københavn #denmark #scandinavia #ukrainianindenmark #copenhagen #visitcopenhagen #girlfromdenmark #fitnessgirl #instatravel#lonelyplanet #жизньвдании #дания #копенгаген #скандинавия #девушкаиздании #блогопутешествиях #блогодании #вокругсвета #самостоятельноепутешествие #турист #путешествия #kongenslyngby #indreby #люблюкопенгаген #gammelstrand

Зеленый шпиль церкви святого Николая, видно с любой точки города. Эта церковь построенна на месте сгоревшей, в результате большого пожара в 1795 году. Построили ее в начале 20 века, кстати, денег на убранство выделил известный меценат и основатель пивной марки #Carlsberg Карл Якобсен. Сейчас здесь находиться центр современного искусства-Kunsthallen Nikolaj

This is DAY 3 of Freedom Music Festival vol. 3 , a MOVIE NIGHT at Husets Biograf and a BONUS
•••
at 19:00 “The Breath Courses Through Us” by Alan Roth is a documentary about the early 1960s avant-garde jazz group, the New York Art Quartet. The film focuses on the group’s 35-year reunion, while reaching back through recollections of their foundations and innovative musical ideas. The film emulates the group’s style of music and challenges to let go of the expectations of documentaries we might have, much like free jazz subverts the traditional structure of jazz. •••
at 21:00 “Rising Tones Cross” by Ebba Jahn will take you in time to NYC of the 80s, a rough-and-tumble place filled with a wonderful array of musicians in a state of hyper-creativity. The film features players like Charles Gayle, William Parker, John Zorn, Jemeel Moondoc, Irene Schweizer or Peter Brötzmann. •••
BONUS: 8:20 PM : Tomo Jacobson + Rasmus Kjærgård Lund 'Solo no. 7' & 'Solo no. 8' release party! A short yet condensed release party, with two solo concerts by Tomo and Rasmus who embarked on a journey to release one solo each month of 2017. Impressive enough.
See you in Husets Biograf.

Danish architecture + Ancient Greece + rationality I : Architecture & design in Denmark convey an outstanding feeling of harmony by their formal rationality and their regularity. The Danish modern era isn't the only one to reach the platonician idea of Beauty : danish neoclassicism from 1800s was directly inspired by Ancient Greece. Doric order from the Church of Our Lady's facade, C.F. Hansen (1817-1829, Copenhagen) #architecture #copenhagen #church #doric #ancientgreece #denmark #danisharchitecture #hansen #indreby #københavn #facade #latinkvarteret

Urbanism + Housing + Infinite III : Nyboder houses by Philip de Lange, 1756. The "functional tradition" and the row houses are two main features of danish housing. The Nyboder district in Copenhagen is the first example of row houses in danish architecture, initiated by Christian IV in 1631. #nyboder #copenhagen #housing #architecture #denmark #danisharchitecture #yellow #indreby #denmark #home

SPICE SPECIALIST 📃

TOP 10 - SMØRREBRØD KBH ❤️ Fik i set mit indlæg vedrørende smørrebrød i København? I har taget så godt imod det, kan jeg jo se på bloggen - men hvis du endnu ikke har læst indlægget, så smut forbi bloggen ❤️. Dette billede er fra et besøg hos @restaurantkronborg . Som i kan se, går de bestemt op i udseender på maden. Og derudover smagte det fantastisk!. Læs mere om Kronborg og de 9 andre steder fra #tourdesmørrebrød ! Rigtig god onsdag! ❤️ Smid endelig en kommentar hvis jeg mangler nogle? .

Lakrids - датчане без ума от него! Это корень солодки. Кажется, это национальный ингридиент. Он может быть соленым и сладким. Добавляют его в самые неожиданные места : в конфеты, в колбасу, в ликер, в шнапс, в чай и кофе. В 2007 Johan Bülow придумал делать шоколадные шарики с различным вкусом, но с обязательным ингридиентом - лакрицей. Сейчас в магазине Magasin в фирменном бутике Lakrids продают мороженое с лакричным вкусом, политое лакричным сладким соусом и присыпанное тёртой лакричной карамелью. Стоит это удовольствие -30 крон -4 евро.

Keratin treatment - 👊🏼👌🏻FRA kruset til lækker glat og glans fuldt👌🏻 Vores Keratin behandling er godkendt af GRØNSalon☘️🙏🏽 Keratin treatment er permanent udglatning som  er fri for formaldehyd, allergener og andre skadelige aldehyder. 
Keratin treatment er til de, som har problemer med krøllet, kruset, bølget og tykt hår, og som ønsker glat, blankt hår, der føles let. 
Keratin treatment efterlader håret , glat✔️ blankt ✔️ frizz frit ✔️ krølle frit ✔️ glans fuldt ✔️lethed ✔️ blødt ✔️ nemt at arbejde med håret ✔️ Gravid kvinder kan også benytte sig af kreatin treatment✔️ Holdbarheden er FRA 3 måneder . 
prieserne kan variere for hver enkel kunde, afhængigt af mængden af hår, hvor meget produkt håret suger og hårets kvalitet. 
Page hår FRA 1500kr
Skulder / skulder langt hår / tykt hår FRA 2200kr
Meget langt hår / tykt hår FRA 2800kr 
Prisen kan ænders ved ekstra behandling. 
Denne behandling kan kun bookes via tlf eller ved personligt frem mødet i salonen .

You might not know it, but Hepcats Copenhagen is a non-profit organisation run solely on the power of our volunteers - be they board members, teachers, DJs, you name it - nobody receives salary for what they do. It is done out of the love for dance and what they can give to the community from their hearts.
We have our annual general assembly coming up on Sunday June 18th at 13.00 at @kulturhusetindreby 
We need a new boost of energy and would love to see new members in the board as we unfortunately are losing a couple of our current members.
Meet up, have your say and join our volunteer family!
Questions? Write to info@swingdans.dk

I samarbejde med performancekunstner @itarpgaard præsenterer vi Walking Workshop under dette års #cphstage. Walking Workshop er en performativ sansevandring i stilhed, hvor man fører andre og lader sig føre gennem det urbane rum. Hverken Tarpgaard eller deltagerne kender retningen for vandringen på forhånd, og det er derfor i mødet mellem tid og sted, oplevelsen skabes.🚶🏻‍♀️🚶🏿🚶🏼🚶🏾‍♀️Link til 🎟 i bio. #ofeliaplads #indreby #performanceart #københavn #voreskbh #kultur #byvandringer #visitcopenhagen

Er det mig der skal lave din næste tattoo, til elevpriser, så skriv i indbakken. 💌

7 nye smykkebrands har set dagens lys!

Alle med én fælles mission; at skabe forandring. Er du nysgerrig efter at se hvilken forandring disse brands kan skabe for netop dig, så kig forbi vores lokaler, hvor en pop-up shop med alle 7 brands vil være at finde frem til og med den 14. maj. 
Vi glæder os til at se dig og hjælper dig gerne med at finde frem til den helt rette forandring for netop dig. 
Så tag en veninde under armen og kig forbi. Shoppen er åben fra kl 11.00-18.00 alle dage.

This old building used to be a bath house (badeanstalten) and was build because people in Copenhagen didn't have shower and toilet facilities in their own appartments. It was placed here because it was very close to the first water work in Copenhagen. Today it's a hotel called Ascot. Right across the street is another old building called Pumpehuset, which means "the pump house". Originally the building was a part of the old water work - today it's a concert venue. #ihavethisthingwithbricks #delditkbh #bricks #bathhouse #1902 #mursten #indreby #studiestræde #pumpehuset #badeanstalten #ascothotelcopenhagen

Ny uge, ny kaffebar! 
Besøgte i dag the Big Apple i Fiolsstræde, stort menukort med kaffe, juice og lidt sandwich. Når man træder ind af den hyggelige dør mødes man af bestillingsbaren og en sindsyg flot og enkel indretning. Der er lidt pladser udenfor til eftermiddagssolen, lidt i stuen og flere ovenpå. Hvis man går op i et lækkert instabillede, er det klart et besøg værd!

Skala 1-5
Kaffe: ☕️☕️☕️☕️ fik iceblend, dejlig kold og  vaniljesmagen var ikke al for sød og passede perfekt til solskinnet.  Arbejdsro: 🤓🤓🤓🤓i top på 1.sal. 
Instapotentiale: 📸📸📸📸📸
Priser: 35-70 kr.

Giv en hilsen til @rikketjustrup 👋
Hun har siden november været frivillig teamleder for Besøgstjenesten i Indre By:
”Jeg ville gerne arbejde frivilligt, og da jeg så Røde Kors Hovedstadens’s opslag om en teamleder for Indre By, sprang jeg til," fortæller hun.
Som teamleder står Rikke blandt andet for at matche frivillige besøgsvenner og besøgsmodtagere:
”Jeg ser generelt et utroligt spændende match, når ældre og unge kan mødes og lære af hinanden - for det går helt sikkert begge veje,” siger hun.
Det er dejligt at have dig med på holdet, Rikke 🙂
Masser af 👍👍👍 til dig for din frivillige indsats! #besøgstjenesten #indreby #frivillig #rødekors #rkhovedstaden

🇩🇰Spring in Copenhagen! 🌷Indre By (lit. English, "Inner City"), also known as Copenhagen Center or K or Downtown Copenhagen, is an administrative district (by) in central Copenhagen, the capital of Denmark. This district is the historic, geographic and political heart of present-day Copenhagen, and reflects the history of Denmark. Its boundaries pretty much reflect the entire city’s extent during the reign of King Christian IV (1588-1648). 👑#springincopenhagen #indreby #storeregnegade #storeregnegade19 #jazzhusmontmartre #copenhagen #københavn #köpenhamn #kopenhagen #denmark #danmark #dänemark #scandinavianlifestyle #scandinavia #visitdenmark #opdagdanmark #voreskbh #kbh

@lakorsoulwear åbnede igår op i vores lokaler

Lidt info om eventet: 🐋 LAKOR X LINTS pop-up KBH 🐋

LAKOR har slæbt et stykke Jylland med til hovedstaden, når vi præsenterer vores kunstudstilling og sommerkollektion, lavet i samarbejde med den Københavnske graffitikunstner, Lints. Partnerskabet er på mange måder et kontrastfyldt sammenstød mellem graffitikunst og tekstildesign, by og hav samt Købehavn og Jylland.
Ud over tøj og kunst, vil der i ugens løb være aktiviteter i butikken:

Program:

Lørdag: Udstilling af billedeserien "Tavaha" fra Gjerluff photography . 
Søndag (02.04.17 ): Lints x LAKOR live kunst.
Tirsdag (04.04.17): Gratis Skipper’s Pipes - Lakridspiben
Fredag (07.04.17): Ginsmagning fra Nordisk Brænderi.
Kig forbi butikken til hvalsafari, unika kunst og lakridspiber. ⚓️🐋🎣 Vi glæder os til at se dig.⚓️🐋🎣 #lakorshop #lakorsoulwear #popupcopenhagen #streetwear #streetart #copenhagen #københavn #graffiti #streetkunst #kunst #sharingcph #delditkbh #aokdk #ibyen #mitkbh #voreskbh #cphpicks #udstilling #popupbutik #teglgårdstræde #larsbjørnsstræde #studiestræde #pisserenden #indreby #indrekøbenhavn
